<p class="kt-adv-heading550_539b7f-3a wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading550_539b7f-3a">Discover detailed guides to Spain’s lesser-known destinations, practical travel advice, cultural insights, and comprehensive language-learning resources.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns550_d1b339-b9"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn550_6a91b8-50 kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-inherit  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-button__link wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://loveatfirstadventure.com/spain-country-guide/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">Explore Travel Guide</span></a>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column550_a44143-fb kb-section-dir-vertical inner-column-1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h6 class="kt-adv-heading550_efa07e-ac wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-1-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading550_efa07e-ac">meet your travel blogger</h6>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading550_8e4475-f3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading550_8e4475-f3">Welcome, I&#8217;m Tristina</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading550_56abc7-51 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading550_56abc7-51">Having <strong>lived in Spain</strong> and traveled through its rich regions for <strong>nearly two decades</strong>, my love for Spanish culture runs deep. From <strong>small-town life</strong> to <strong>solo road trips</strong> and the <strong><a href="https://loveatfirstadventure.com/camino-de-santiago-guide/">Camino de Santiago</a></strong>, I&#8217;m here to share my passion and knowledge with you!</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading550_e4f3c9-c3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading550_e4f3c9-c3">An ex-Spanish teacher, I also use this blog to share my best tips and tricks for learning Spanish.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading550_1021b3-64 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading550_1021b3-64"><strong>Ready to immerse yourself in Spain&#8217;s way of life?</strong> Explore the site for personal insights, or <strong><a href="https://loveatfirstadventure.com/about-tristina/">click to learn more.</a></strong></p>

<h4 class="kt-adv-heading550_fca73f-1c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-2-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading550_fca73f-1c">Inquiry</h4>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading550_93e67c-9c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading550_93e67c-9c">Let’s create youR Spain itinerary</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading550_64ef83-6e wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading550_64ef83-6e"><strong>Interested in a <a href="https://loveatfirstadventure.com/custom-spain-itinerary/" data-type="page" data-id="19869">custom Spain itinerary</a>?</strong> Send us a message at <strong>tristina@loveatfirstadventure.com</strong> with where you&#8217;d like to go, travel dates, # of travelers, budget, and other pertinent details. We&#8217;ll get back to you within 48 hours.</p>
